comprehensive three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) across the following key components:\\n\\n## 1. Role Type Definitions\\n\\nThe fundamental role types are defined in **pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go** (RoleType, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, RoleAdmin) with a precedence system where Admin > Editor > Viewer > None. The RoleType includes:\\n- `Includes()` method to check role hierarchy\\n- `Children()` and `Parents()` methods for role relationships  \\n- `rolePrecedence` map defining precedence values (10-40)\\n\\nThese are aliased in **pkg/services/org/model.go** for organizational context.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\nThe core role-to-permission mapping is established in **pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go**:\\n\\n- **BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()**: Creates the three basic roles (Admin, Editor, Viewer) with UIDs like \\\"basic_admin\\\", \\\"basic_editor\\\", \\\"basic_viewer\\\"\\n- **DeclareFixedRoles()**: Registers roles and their permission grants\\n- Uses prefixes: \\\"basic:\\\" for basic roles, \\\"fixed:\\\" for fixed roles, \\\"managed:\\\" for managed roles\\n\\nResource-specific action mappings are defined in:\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go**:\\n- `DashboardViewActions`: READ permissions\\n- `DashboardEditActions`: READ + WRITE + DELETE permissions  \\n- `DashboardAdminActions`: READ + WRITE + DELETE + PERMISSIONS READ/WRITE\\n- `registerDashboardRoles()`: Declares dashboard roles for each tier\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go**:\\n- `FolderViewActions`: READ, ALERTING_READ, LIBRARY_READ, SILENCES_READ\\n- `FolderEditActions`: VIEW + WRITE + DELETE + CREATE dashboards + alerting rules\\n- `FolderAdminActions`: EDIT + PERMISSIONS READ/WRITE\\n- `registerFolderRoles()`: Declares folder roles for each tier\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\nPermission enforcement is implemented through middleware layers:\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go**:\\n- `Middleware()`: Core permission checking middleware that evaluates actions against user permissions\\n- `authorize()`: Executes evaluator and denies access if evaluation fails\\n- `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()`: Validates user has permissions in target organization\\n- Uses scope injection and mutation for dynamic scopes\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/middleware.go**:\\n- `ReqEditorRole`: Middleware for Editor+Admin role requirement\\n- `ReqOrgAdmin`: Middleware for Admin-only requirement\\n- Basic role authentication middleware definitions\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/auth.go**:\\n- `RoleAuth()`: Simple middleware checking if user's OrgRole matches required roles\\n- Uses `c.OrgRole` to check against allowed roles\\n- `Auth()`: Authentication options middleware\\n- `SnapshotPublicModeOrCreate()`, `SnapshotPublicModeOrDelete()`: Conditional permission checks\\n\\n## 4. Permission Evaluation System\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go**:\\n- `Evaluator` interface: Defines permission evaluation contract\\n- `EvalPermission()`: Creates evaluator checking specific action+scopes\\n- `EvalAll()`: Creates evaluator requiring all sub-evaluators pass\\n- `permissionEvaluator.Evaluate()`: Checks if user permissions match required action/scopes\\n- Implements wildcard matching for scope patterns (e.g., \\\"folders:*\\\")\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `Evaluate()`: Core access control evaluation method\\n- Evaluates permissions after resolving scopes\\n- Handles scope resolution via ScopeAttributeResolvers\\n\\n## 5. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\nPermission inheritance through folder hierarchy:\\n\\n**pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `GetInheritedScopes()`: Retrieves parent folder scopes for a resource\\n  - Calls `folderSvc.GetParents()` to traverse ancestor folders\\n  - Returns scopes for all ancestor folders in the hierarchy\\n  - Returns nil for General folder (no inheritance)\\n- `NewFolderUIDScopeResolver()`: Scope resolver that includes folder + all ancestor scopes\\n- `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()`: Dashboard resolver that includes folder hierarchy\\n- `resolveDashboardScope()`: Returns dashboard + folder + ancestor scopes for evaluation\\n\\n**pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go**:\\n- `GetParents()` query: Retrieves ancestor folders for a given folder UID\\n- Folder permissions are inherited from parent folders\\n- Comments in code: \\\"if the parent is accessible then the subfolders are accessible as well (due to inheritance)\\\"\\n\\n**pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder_unifiedstorage.go**:\\n- `getAvailableNonRootFolders()`: Filters folders based on user's folder and dashboard permissions\\n- Combines parent folder permissions with dashboard permissions\\n- Handles permission hierarchy: EDIT permissions include READ permissions\\n\\n## 6. Authorization Model\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/authorizer.go**:\\n- `ResourceResolver`: Interface for translating resources to scopes\\n- `LegacyAccessClient`: Maps K8s verbs to RBAC actions\\n- Default mapping: Get→read, Create→create, Update→write, Delete→delete, SetPermissions→permissions:write\\n\\n**pkg/api/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `declareFixedRoles()`: Declares all fixed roles for API operations\\n- Registers roles with their grants to basic org roles\\n- Defines permissions for provisioning, datasources, and other API operations\\n\\n## 7. Scope Model\\n\\nScopes provide fine-grained resource access:\\n- Format: \\\"resource:uid:value\\\" (e.g., \\\"dashboards:uid:my-dashboard\\\", \\\"folders:uid:my-folder\\\")\\n- Wildcards: \\\"folders:*\\\" matches all folders\\n- Providers: ScopeFoldersProvider, ScopeDashboardsProvider for scope generation\\n- Scope hierarchy respects folder/dashboard relationships\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe three-tier permission model flows as:\\n\\n1. **Type Definition**: RoleType enum (pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go)\\n2. **Role Creation**: BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() in roles.go creates Admin/Editor/Viewer\\n3. **Action Mapping**: registerDashboardRoles/registerFolderRoles map actions to roles\\n4. **Middleware Enforcement**: RoleAuth/Middleware in middleware packages check org role\\n5. **Permission Evaluation**: EvalPermission/Evaluate checks actions+scopes against user permissions\\n6. **Inheritance**: GetInheritedScopes includes parent folder scopes in evaluation\\n7. **Authorization**: AccessControl.Evaluate executes the full permission check with scope resolution\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3110,"cache_read_input_tokens":99090,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3110},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"82d57ae8-1901-4faa-91a3-1c72f778ffb6","uuid":"33570106-ef99-4fc5-9aee-382520bc1c40"}

comprehensive three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) across the following key components:\\n\\n## 1. Role Type Definitions\\n\\nThe fundamental role types are defined in **pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go** (RoleType, RoleViewer, RoleEditor, RoleAdmin) with a precedence system where Admin > Editor > Viewer > None. The RoleType includes:\\n- `Includes()` method to check role hierarchy\\n- `Children()` and `Parents()` methods for role relationships  \\n- `rolePrecedence` map defining precedence values (10-40)\\n\\nThese are aliased in **pkg/services/org/model.go** for organizational context.\\n\\n## 2. Role-to-Permission Mapping\\n\\nThe core role-to-permission mapping is established in **pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go**:\\n\\n- **BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()**: Creates the three basic roles (Admin, Editor, Viewer) with UIDs like \\\"basic_admin\\\", \\\"basic_editor\\\", \\\"basic_viewer\\\"\\n- **DeclareFixedRoles()**: Registers roles and their permission grants\\n- Uses prefixes: \\\"basic:\\\" for basic roles, \\\"fixed:\\\" for fixed roles, \\\"managed:\\\" for managed roles\\n\\nResource-specific action mappings are defined in:\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/dashboard.go**:\\n- `DashboardViewActions`: READ permissions\\n- `DashboardEditActions`: READ + WRITE + DELETE permissions  \\n- `DashboardAdminActions`: READ + WRITE + DELETE + PERMISSIONS READ/WRITE\\n- `registerDashboardRoles()`: Declares dashboard roles for each tier\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/ossaccesscontrol/folder.go**:\\n- `FolderViewActions`: READ, ALERTING_READ, LIBRARY_READ, SILENCES_READ\\n- `FolderEditActions`: VIEW + WRITE + DELETE + CREATE dashboards + alerting rules\\n- `FolderAdminActions`: EDIT + PERMISSIONS READ/WRITE\\n- `registerFolderRoles()`: Declares folder roles for each tier\\n\\n## 3. Permission Guard Middleware\\n\\nPermission enforcement is implemented through middleware layers:\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/middleware.go**:\\n- `Middleware()`: Core permission checking middleware that evaluates actions against user permissions\\n- `authorize()`: Executes evaluator and denies access if evaluation fails\\n- `AuthorizeInOrgMiddleware()`: Validates user has permissions in target organization\\n- Uses scope injection and mutation for dynamic scopes\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/middleware.go**:\\n- `ReqEditorRole`: Middleware for Editor+Admin role requirement\\n- `ReqOrgAdmin`: Middleware for Admin-only requirement\\n- Basic role authentication middleware definitions\\n\\n**pkg/middleware/auth.go**:\\n- `RoleAuth()`: Simple middleware checking if user's OrgRole matches required roles\\n- Uses `c.OrgRole` to check against allowed roles\\n- `Auth()`: Authentication options middleware\\n- `SnapshotPublicModeOrCreate()`, `SnapshotPublicModeOrDelete()`: Conditional permission checks\\n\\n## 4. Permission Evaluation System\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/evaluator.go**:\\n- `Evaluator` interface: Defines permission evaluation contract\\n- `EvalPermission()`: Creates evaluator checking specific action+scopes\\n- `EvalAll()`: Creates evaluator requiring all sub-evaluators pass\\n- `permissionEvaluator.Evaluate()`: Checks if user permissions match required action/scopes\\n- Implements wildcard matching for scope patterns (e.g., \\\"folders:*\\\")\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/acimpl/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `Evaluate()`: Core access control evaluation method\\n- Evaluates permissions after resolving scopes\\n- Handles scope resolution via ScopeAttributeResolvers\\n\\n## 5. Folder/Dashboard Permission Inheritance\\n\\nPermission inheritance through folder hierarchy:\\n\\n**pkg/services/dashboards/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `GetInheritedScopes()`: Retrieves parent folder scopes for a resource\\n  - Calls `folderSvc.GetParents()` to traverse ancestor folders\\n  - Returns scopes for all ancestor folders in the hierarchy\\n  - Returns nil for General folder (no inheritance)\\n- `NewFolderUIDScopeResolver()`: Scope resolver that includes folder + all ancestor scopes\\n- `NewDashboardUIDScopeResolver()`: Dashboard resolver that includes folder hierarchy\\n- `resolveDashboardScope()`: Returns dashboard + folder + ancestor scopes for evaluation\\n\\n**pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder.go**:\\n- `GetParents()` query: Retrieves ancestor folders for a given folder UID\\n- Folder permissions are inherited from parent folders\\n- Comments in code: \\\"if the parent is accessible then the subfolders are accessible as well (due to inheritance)\\\"\\n\\n**pkg/services/folder/folderimpl/folder_unifiedstorage.go**:\\n- `getAvailableNonRootFolders()`: Filters folders based on user's folder and dashboard permissions\\n- Combines parent folder permissions with dashboard permissions\\n- Handles permission hierarchy: EDIT permissions include READ permissions\\n\\n## 6. Authorization Model\\n\\n**pkg/services/accesscontrol/authorizer.go**:\\n- `ResourceResolver`: Interface for translating resources to scopes\\n- `LegacyAccessClient`: Maps K8s verbs to RBAC actions\\n- Default mapping: Get→read, Create→create, Update→write, Delete→delete, SetPermissions→permissions:write\\n\\n**pkg/api/accesscontrol.go**:\\n- `declareFixedRoles()`: Declares all fixed roles for API operations\\n- Registers roles with their grants to basic org roles\\n- Defines permissions for provisioning, datasources, and other API operations\\n\\n## 7. Scope Model\\n\\nScopes provide fine-grained resource access:\\n- Format: \\\"resource:uid:value\\\" (e.g., \\\"dashboards:uid:my-dashboard\\\", \\\"folders:uid:my-folder\\\")\\n- Wildcards: \\\"folders:*\\\" matches all folders\\n- Providers: ScopeFoldersProvider, ScopeDashboardsProvider for scope generation\\n- Scope hierarchy respects folder/dashboard relationships\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe three-tier permission model flows as:\\n\\n1. **Type Definition**: RoleType enum (pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go)\\n2. **Role Creation**: BuildBasicRoleDefinitions() in roles.go creates Admin/Editor/Viewer\\n3. **Action Mapping**: registerDashboardRoles/registerFolderRoles map actions to roles\\n4. **Middleware Enforcement**: RoleAuth/Middleware in middleware packages check org role\\n5. **Permission Evaluation**: EvalPermission/Evaluate checks actions+scopes against user permissions\\n6. **Inheritance**: GetInheritedScopes includes parent folder scopes in evaluation\\n7. **Authorization**: AccessControl.Evaluate executes the full permission check with scope resolution\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
